Local News

International Telegraph Office Tested Sino-British Telegram Communication Yesterday 164

Excellent Results and Opening at the Beginning of the Month

Implement Formal Commercial Telegrams

Huadong News Agency reports that the direct Sino-British telegram communication from Shanghai to London, since the Ministry of Communications and the British Transport Company began preparing for it in April of last year, has been working hard to implement it. Now, all the large and small machines ordered from the UK arrived in Shanghai at the end of last year. The International Telegraph Office sent personnel to install the radio station project. As of the previous day, all the projects, such as antennas, transceivers, and small machines, have been installed. Other equipment is also complete. This great international communication work has been completed.

Yesterday's Test Report 165

The International Telegraph Office held a test report with the United Kingdom yesterday. At 3 p.m., Zhang Chenghu, Director of the Receiving and Dispatching Office of the International Radio Station of the bureau, personally conducted the test report at the receiving and dispatching office in Sassoon House. He began the power generation work on the transceiver. After passing through the Zhenru Radio Station, it went directly to London, England. Power generation lasted for an hour, and stopped at 4 p.m.

Excellent Results 166

It is said that the results of yesterday's test report were quite good. According to a Huadong News Agency reporter, London time is eight hours earlier than Shanghai. Therefore, when the receiving and dispatching office held the test report yesterday, it was 7 a.m. in London, England. The British side paid attention to the wavelength, sound band, speed, etc., issued from here, and scheduled to draft a report on the results of the power generation from here to there at 11 p.m. last night to inform Shanghai by telegram. In order to be cautious, the International Telegraph Office plans to hold this test report for a week to explore whether there are any shortcomings in the project that can be improved.

Preparing for the Opening 167

After a week of test reports starting yesterday, the International Telegraph Office has submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications to approve the opening date. At the same time, the bureau is also preparing for the opening procedures. After the opening, it can formally start sending commercial telegrams. The estimated opening date is expected to be at the beginning of next month.

Telegram Overview 168

The Ministry of Communications has had this intention for Sino-British telegram communication from Shanghai to London since the summer of the year before last. At that time, it convened telecommunications experts from the ministry to discuss the outline of this method. After the decision, it signed a contract with the British Transport Company and purchased telecommunications equipment from that country. In April of last year, the Ministry of Communications ordered the International Telegraph Office to engage in the construction of a radio station project in Zhenru. By the winter of last year, all the machines required for the radio station had been shipped from England to Shanghai. At this point, the Telegraph Office more actively carried out installation work, and all the work was completed recently. The total cost of the equipment reached 64,000 pounds sterling. According to the recent market price, each pound is equivalent to 16 yuan in national currency, totaling more than one million yuan. The installation costs are not included.

Meeting Order 176

㈠ All stand at attention, ㈡ Sing the party song, ㈣ Bow to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Generalissimo, ㈣ The chairman respectfully reads the Generalissimo's will, ㈤ Observe three minutes of silence, ㈥ Chairman's report, ㈦ Speeches, ㈧ Proposals, ㈨ Shout slogans, ㈩ Adjournment.

Chairman's Report 177

Chairman Yu Jiayong reported, roughly saying, "Fellow comrades, fellow representatives, the significance of holding today's anti-rebellion rally is that our sailors should understand that this rebellion in Fujian is a crime of endangering the Republic of China and ruining the nation. Now that the central government's campaign against the rebellion is winning victory after victory, our sailors should indirectly and directly help the central government to eliminate the rebellion. Today's crisis in China is more serious than at any time in the past, and a few unstable elements entrenched in Fujian, such as Li Jishen and Chen Mingshu, want to satisfy their private desires and do not hesitate to go against the tide of history, willingly selling the life of the Chinese nation and creating this absurd pseudo-organization. This is indeed the same as the rebellious and traitorous acts of Yuan Shikai, Chen Jiongming, and others, and their crimes are punishable. The first result of their rebellion is to give Japan a good opportunity to invade China. Japan's invasion of China is not limited to the Northeast, and all coastal provinces are within the scope of Japanese invasion. Foreign forces often use brainless and opinionless warlords to create chaos in China. This Fujian Incident is no exception. Second, because today China wants social stability and the smooth progress of national construction, the premise is to eliminate the Red bandits. Now the central government is surrounding and blockading the Red bandits in Jiangxi, and it is not difficult to say that they will be wiped out in a short period of time. However, the rebels in Fujian have given the Red bandits the rice and salt they need to prolong their lives as an exchange condition for not infringing on each other, and have provided the Red bandits with a place to cause trouble in western Fujian. Therefore, all the people of the country, as long as they understand right and wrong and have opinions, cannot bear to see the rebellious Fujian act of ruining the nation and the country. Therefore, all localities have requested the central government to send troops to suppress the rebellion. The inevitable process of revolution is that first, there must be a sincere spirit; second, there must be methods; and third, there must be a theory. The rebels in Fujian, Li Jishen, Chen Mingshu, etc., have forced public opinion to satisfy their ambitions, have long betrayed the revolutionary stance, and have deviated from the revolutionary reality. They have put forward many slogans, such as 'land to the tiller,' which are actually deceiving the people. Our party's land policy has very concrete methods in the writings of the late Premier Sun, which show us that the so-called 'land to the tiller' of the rebels is not feasible in theory or in fact. Therefore, this rebellion is bound to collapse. However, after this rebellion, not only will the vitality of Fujian be greatly lost, but the impact on the whole country will not be small." After the chairman's report, Chen Songping, secretary of the Seamen's Party Department, and others continued to speak, and the words were omitted for brevity.

The Second Anniversary of the "January 28th Incident" is Approaching 184

All Sectors Prepare for a Memorial Service

Dagong News Agency reported that the blood of the martyred compatriots has not yet dried, the battlefield is tragic, and the situation is still there. The second anniversary of the Japanese invaders' trampling on Shanghai during the January 28th Incident is approaching. The Shanghai Municipal Party Department, in order to stimulate the patriotic thinking of the people and never forget the destruction by the enemy, has convened all sectors to prepare for an expanded memorial service. Military and police agencies will also jointly announce special precautions on that day.

Expanded Memorial 185

The second anniversary of the January 28th Incident is only fifteen days away. The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department has specifically decided to convene all sectors at the Diplomatic Building on Fenglin Bridge at 9 am on that day to hold an expanded memorial service. In the afternoon, it will send a letter to the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant, requesting the dispatch of aircraft to distribute a letter to all citizens in the sky over the city, informing citizens to fly a half-mast in mourning for the compatriots who died in the January 28th Incident, to avenge their shame and strengthen themselves. It is also scheduled to convene the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, the Municipal Farmers' Association, the Municipal Citizens' Federation, the Municipal Education Association, and the Student Federation and other groups next week to hold a preparatory meeting to discuss the implementation plan.

Special Precautions 186

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, the Garrison Command, the Security Office, and other military and police agencies, because the second anniversary of the January 28th Shanghai War is approaching, and it is a time of tense situation, fear that reactionary elements will take the opportunity to cause trouble and serious incidents. Therefore, it has been decided to jointly announce special precautions from 8 am on that day. The Municipal Public Security Bureau has instructed all district offices under its jurisdiction to take strict precautions, and secretly ordered the Zhabei and Wusong districts to increase the number of patrol police by four at the border areas where Japanese residents and troops are concentrated, to strictly prevent traitors from causing trouble.

Jianghai Customs Notice Restricting Ship Workers from Selling Copper Coins 188

Each person is limited to one thousand coins.

In order to prevent the smuggling of copper coins, the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance has stipulated restrictions and ordered the Jianghai Customs to comply. It is learned that Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Borel, Customs Officer, specially issued Notice No. 1333 yesterday, stating that "In accordance with the order of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, ship workers carrying copper coins, whether on ships from domestic or foreign ports, are uniformly limited to one thousand single copper coins per person per trip." This notice is hereby issued for all ship workers to comply with.

The Second Step in the Plan to Prosper the New Urban Area 189

Decision to Complete the Qiujiang Wharf 190

Pay attention to Public Security and Traffic and Prepare a Model Police District

Welcome Financial and Industrial Circles to Invest Actively

Hold a Special Meeting within Two Weeks to Determine the Direction

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that since the municipal government moved into the central urban area, its first step, led by the municipal authorities, has been realized in order to guide citizens to work together in the construction of a new Shanghai. Therefore, Wu Tiecheng, the mayor, proposed a report on the beginning of the second step plan at the municipal meeting yesterday morning, which has been determined to have a plan, and immediately ordered the responsible departments to prepare a detailed plan report within two weeks for submission, so as to hold another special meeting to determine the direction. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency met with Secretary-General Yu Hongjun yesterday and received a very detailed report, which is specially recorded as follows:

Model Police District 191

According to Secretary-General Yu's statement, since the mayor moved the municipal government into the central urban area, he has paid extraordinary attention to the efforts to prosper the central urban area. Therefore, at the municipal meeting on the important day (yesterday), he proposed a plan to continue to build the central urban area, and believed that the prosperity of a city should first pay attention to the two problems of public security and traffic. Therefore, in terms of public security, it has been decided to establish a model police district in the central urban area, which will be ordered by the Municipal Public Security Bureau to conduct detailed research and prepare a plan report for submission for selection. However, after the establishment in the future, whether its affiliation will still belong to the scope of the Public Security Bureau or directly to the municipal government still needs to be finally decided.

Qiujiang Wharf 192

Secondly, the prosperity of the central urban area is most closely related to the construction of the Qiujiang Wharf. Shanghai is a major trading port, with ships coming and going and masts gathering like clouds. If there is no wharf for berthing, cargo transportation will be difficult to load and unload, and commerce will not be able to prosper. Therefore, the Qiujiang Wharf occupies the most important page in the realization of the Greater Shanghai Plan. Therefore, after the mayor proposed a discussion at today's meeting, he has decided to order the Finance and Public Works Bureaus to immediately follow the previously proposed plan, take a further step, prepare all practical and effective measures, and submit them to the municipal government for decision, so that they can be realized as soon as possible.

Welcome Investment 193

In addition, the mayor believes that the construction of a city is limited if it relies solely on the power of the government. It must have the support of the whole people, with active investment from the financial and industrial circles. Therefore, in the plan, the municipal government welcomes citizens to actively invest in all construction in the central urban area. The municipal government will formulate investment methods and officially announce them.

Special Meeting 194

The above three plans are limited to the responsible departments to prepare them completely within two weeks and report them to the municipal government for collection and discussion. After the departments report, the municipal government will hold a special meeting within two weeks to propose a discussion and decide on the direction of progress.

Songhu Branch Line 195

Secretary-General Yu then talked about other municipal situations, saying that the water and electricity problems in the central urban area have been completely completed since the municipal government moved in, and the post office was also officially established a few days ago. As for the future round-road buses in the central urban area, the tram plan in the north and south cities, the power grid plan, and the Songhu branch line and other issues, they will be gradually realized, taking into account the priority and urgency and the financial resources. However, the construction of the Qiujiang Wharf is currently the top priority, so the goal is to achieve the completion of the project first.

Rushing to Build Housing 196

As for the construction of residential areas in the central urban area, more than 40 mu of land have been taken away since the municipal government valued and distributed them twice. More than 30 residential buildings built by the Xingye Trust Company have already started construction and can be completely completed by the end of April this year. The citizens who have taken the land have recently been taking out donation certificates from the Public Works Bureau and will start construction in the short term. The Shanghai and China banks will start construction soon. Later, the reporter passed by the residential area built by the Xingye Trust Company and saw that the four walls were already firm and were being rushed to build.

Financial Issues 197

He continued, "The city's finances have not yet recovered to the state before the January 28th Incident. However, we are living within our means and cutting expenses as much as possible, so we are not too tight. The Finance Bureau will have a detailed report on the details within the day. Although we wanted to create an unprecedented precedent for education funding this time, there were arrears. But now the Finance Bureau is trying its best to raise funds, and it can be allocated soon. As for the fund for the construction of the central urban area, it is still kept independently. It was not used even when the city's finances were so difficult during the January 28th Incident."

Improving Office Work 198

Secretary-General Yu also said that since the municipal government moved into the new building, it has been felt that the past official documents were cumbersome and complicated, and every official matter had to go through many procedures before it could be completed, which was time-consuming and laborious, and was not conducive to work efficiency. Therefore, since this year, in order to increase efficiency and speed, all official documents have been simplified, and the responsible departments will handle them according to the nature of each event, except for those that must be personally reviewed by the mayor and secretary-general. In addition, the municipal government and various bureaus have also newly formulated measures for contact and negotiation, whether they have moved or not, in order to be quick and convenient.

Indian Bites Off Part of Chinese Man's Ear 199

Sentenced to Two Months in Prison

Indian Laxin was accused of fighting with Chinese shoemaker Hu and biting off part of Hu's ear. The British Consulate Police Department opened a trial on Wednesday and questioned witnesses. A court hearing was reopened a few days ago to continue questioning witnesses about what they saw at the time. Then he asked the defendant why Hu's ear was missing a part. The defendant replied that Hu had probably cut it off himself or asked his friend to do so in order to sue him. Therefore, the interrogator ruled that the reason for the case was that the two sides had different opinions, but in any case, the defendant should not have bitten off part of the person's ear, so he should be sentenced to two months in prison.

A Poor Man Freezes to Death 200

Li Binggen, a farmer from the Li family in Hongqiao Town, West Shanghai, is 36 years old. Because he was addicted to opium, he sold all his family property. He was once detained in the Caohejing Vagrant Work Center and imprisoned for one year. After his release, he relapsed. His wife, Chen, repeatedly advised him not to listen. Two years ago, he divorced Li and sought another life. Binggen was alone from then on and had no choice but to steal things outside. His neighbors hated him to the bone. Recently, due to the severe cold, he collapsed from hunger and cold under a poplar tree beside the back door of Li A'hu on the night before last. Chen, thinking of the relationship between husband and wife, collected his body on his behalf yesterday.

Staff of the Parcel Department of the Directorate General of Posts Use Canceled Stamps for Profit 205

Prosecuted After Being Discovered by Inspectors

Chen Kesheng, a native of Wenzhou and an employee of the Parcel Department of the Directorate General of Posts on North Suzhou Road, used canceled stamps for profit between October 22 last year and January 9 this year. Recently, he was discovered by Ge Fei, an inspector of the bureau, and reported to the postmaster. The Hongkou Police Station was dispatched on the previous day to send Chinese and Western detectives to arrest Chen and take him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The lawyer of the police station, Yu Yaotang, stated that the defendant was in charge of a large number of postal items such as various books and leaflets sent to other ports. According to the regulations, a triplicate book was used, which was of three types: A, B, and C. The Ai character was for the stub, the Pi character was pasted on the package, and the Xi character was for the receipt for the customer. The number of such documents was quite large, and the defendant had to estimate the number of stamps to be affixed. He secretly took down the stamps covered with seals on the Pi character package, used fraud to alter them, and pasted them on the triplicate book, which could be reused as a receipt for the customer's Xi character, and profited from it. He was discovered by Inspector Ge. He went to the World Bookstore, a postal customer, and brought back the receipt. When comparing it with the triplicate book, the stamps were inconsistent. When he questioned the defendant, he denied it. He immediately checked the number of tickets sold and calculated that it was 805 yuan, 1 dime and 7 cents. Because the bureau issued stamps every time to the tune of 800 yuan, and would pay again after they were sold out, there was never a large number. At this point, he admitted that each time he committed fraud, it was only tens of yuan. It is difficult to find out the exact amount of money he took in this way. Please investigate and deal with it severely to warn others. He then presented a bundle of triplicate receipts. Then, the inspector testified about the process and said that the defendant had been working in the bureau for ten years and his monthly salary was 90 yuan. When asked about the defendant, he stammered and said that he was confused for a while and took this unwise measure, and it only lasted for three months. Please forgive him. Judge Xiao Fenfen ordered him to be remanded in custody and scheduled a sentence.

Crane Injures Two Workers 206

The Japanese Qing Company's Lusong Maru ship was loading bran to Taiwan. At about 7:15 last night, the barge was transporting goods onto the ship. The ship had a crane, which could hold 30 bags of bran each time, weighing about 2,000 pounds. Suddenly, the hook on the top broke, and a large amount of bran was pressed down, hitting two small workers, Yang Shaojiao and Yao Chunfu. Yang's legs were broken, and Yao was injured in the head, waist, and other parts. The situation was very serious. They were sent to the Tongren Hospital for treatment in a car.

Several Questions Regarding the Choice of Subjects to Study 219

| Discussion on the subjects selected by readers in applications, letters, and questionnaires |

We have a clearer understanding of the readers' "desire to study" and "personal circumstances" from the returned "questionnaires," "applications," and letters, but we still feel vague about the readers' "purpose of studying," and the subjects selected are also lacking in a system, not very suitable, and some readers even only know that they want to study but don't know why, and only know that they want to learn a major, but don't know which one. In the "What subject do you want to study now" column in the application form, some people even wrote "Lost in the sea of learning, I don't know what to choose, but I urgently hope to have a major to study" without filling in a subject; Most of the others have filled in the subjects they want to study, but if we make a guidance or a "research method" according to their subjects, we can conclude that the effect is probably limited. Because the subjects filled in are either too many, or these subjects are too specialized to be studied, or they are not suitable for their needs: In short, the subjects they have chosen, according to our knowledge of the readers' environment, cannot be appropriately coordinated with their life situation:

Regarding the "purpose of studying," we have repeatedly stated in "On Self-Study" and "The Reading Guidance We Need," namely, "We are for the sake of practicality, to understand actual life, and how to struggle to develop our own or the public's life." and "Reading is a means, not an end." Although the purpose stated by the readers does not fundamentally conflict with ours, it is too general to say "to understand the content of the book to get rich knowledge" or to say "to get considerable knowledge." Therefore, first, we hope that readers have a deep understanding of the "purpose of studying."

Most of our readers, that is, those who participate in "reading guidance," are young shop assistants, office workers, apprentices, and employees of various other enterprises. Their education is about the level of higher primary school or junior high school, their income is usually mostly between 20 and 30 yuan, and their reading time is only one or two hours on average. We know that it is not practical to want to study Einstein's theory of relativity without even understanding elementary algebra; to want to study five or six subjects with only one or two hours of leisure every day; or to hope to prepare a lot of money to buy books when even life can only be勉强maintain. Therefore, we only hope that they can acquire sufficient common sense about what they want to study. As for whether they will become scholars or experts, it depends on their personal efforts and their environment. We don't think so. (To be continued)

Letters 220

Dear Editor, I am writing to you regarding a news report in your newspaper on January 11, stating that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has officially taken over two sea vessels after the Central Army's victory in Fujian. After investigation, the price of the two vessels is to be paid in installments, and the payment period has not yet expired, so they have not been taken over. Moreover, after the price is paid in full, obtaining a nationality certificate and registering the ownership in accordance with the Ship Law are all procedures that should be handled in accordance with maritime administration, and have nothing to do with the Central Army's victory in Fujian. I am writing to request a correction. Sincerely, The General Manager's Office of the State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, January 12.

Dear Editor, The news about the labor dispute at Meifeng Silk Factory, as reported in your newspaper's New Year's Joint Special Issue and in recent days, is inconsistent with the facts and lacks accuracy. After investigation, the factory's capital is 50,000 yuan in total. Since its establishment, there has been a slight surplus, but it has since declined and has suffered a net loss of approximately 200,000 yuan in recent years, which is more than four times the amount of capital. All assets are mortgaged to the hilt. Mr. Ni Dachun, the founder of the factory, is enthusiastic about industry and has not dared to lag behind others. However, due to the impact of the silk industry's bankruptcy, he was unable to save the situation and had no choice but to close the business. His pain is greater than that of the workers. He definitely did not close the business to protect his capital. The books are all there and cannot be concealed. When the closure was announced, workers Li Xichun and Wang Xianyue made a loud noise and were taken to the police station for questioning by the police officers present, and were immediately released. This was a matter of the police officers' authority and did not involve our client. Entrusted by our client, we are writing to present the facts and request that they be published immediately for correction. Respectfully, Lawyer Jiang Baoli, January 12, 23rd year.

Spring and Autumn

Father Lu's "Cheat" Zhan Lu 221

Since the Republic of China, many important figures in the military and political circles have become monks. In the past, there was Cheng Xuelou; in modern times, there was Sun Xinyuan; others, such as Duan Zhiqian, are even more countless. It is not surprising that they have become Chinese monks; what is most surprising is that Mr. Lu Zhengxiang, who served as the Prime Minister and Minister of Foreign Affairs in the early years of the Republic of China, served as the Chinese Chief Representative at the Paris Peace Conference in the eighth year of the Republic of China, and served as the Chinese Minister to Switzerland in the eleventh year of the Republic of China, is now a foreign-style monk, wearing ancient clothes and hats, vowing to cultivate in a monastery in Belgium, spending a lonely life in the ancient temple bells. From the sixteenth year of the Republic of China to this year, it has been seven or eight years, which is truly a special figure in the history of the Republic of China.

Recently, someone went to the monastery to visit Mr. Lu, the former Prime Minister and now a priest, and asked him about his feelings about the ancestral country. He said: "The world is a deception; China is a country of deception; the family is a family where family members and fathers deceive each other; society is a society where relatives and friends deceive each other; in the former Qing Dynasty, promotion and wealth were deceptive banners; in the Republic of China, personal territory is the deceptive goal; the former exploited the people; the latter exploits them even more. I have been an official in the former Qing Dynasty and worked in the Republic of China. I am also one of the cheaters in the country of deception; however, now I have jumped out of the shackles of deception and restored my natural face."

Father Lu's "cheat" is unusually incisive. In an era of rampant human desires, hearing him talk about cheating can really be compared to a dose of cooling powder. What other irreconcilable hatred is there? Alas! Knowing that it is all a deception, why bother to waste your form, waste your spirit, increase your sins, and arouse your ambitions? Unfortunately, until the appropriate time comes, no one will admit that they are one of the cheaters! No one is willing to jump out of the shackles of cheating! No one is willing to restore my natural face! Then the world will be troubled from then on.

The world is inherently peaceful, but cheaters disturb it themselves.

Bumping into Nails Xie Chengxun 222

The term "bumping into nails" is often associated with the term "bad luck"; because in the minds of ordinary people, it is believed that "bumping into nails" is the cause, and "bad luck" is the effect. Because "bad luck" is what most people, especially those who call themselves modern, are most unwilling to do, so "bumping into nails" is equally despised by people.

In fact, in the current society, which is full of thorns, there are too many opportunities for people to "bump into nails." If you can have a proper understanding of it, you can regard "bumping into nails" as not a big deal; However, most people nowadays, especially young students, have never tasted the feeling of "bumping into nails" in school. When they leave school and enter society, they think it is "bad luck" when they "bump" into "nails." From this, they feel that society is always evil, and reduce most of their courage to work hard for society in the past, or even become negative, pessimistic, decadent, and slowly embark on the road of "taking care of themselves," causing a great crisis in the future of society.

Since "bumping into nails" is an inevitable fact in the current society, I think we should not despise "bumping into nails," nor should we be afraid of "bumping into nails," and we should not think that "bumping into nails" is "bad luck"; and we need to view "bumping into nails" as follows: "Bumping" into "nails" once increases one point of knowledge, the more "nails" are "bumped" into, the more you can have a deep understanding of the ways of the world and human relationships; in other words: the more you can approach the road to success, so I personally welcome "bumping into nails," and I hope my comrades have more!

Starting from Hugging the Quilt Yu Renwei 223

People seem to be especially good at sleeping in winter. The young masters and ladies of Hillchoya almost all have the habit of "not getting out of bed until after lunch"; anyway, the school is on holiday, and someone at home takes care of everything, so they are happy to stay in the quilt for a while.

Not to mention rich people, even us poor kids have felt these days that it is really an unusually painful and difficult thing to get up and get dressed in the cold weather, something that only a great hero can do. Sometimes I also recite the sentence "Get up at dawn" in Mr. Zhu Bolu's Family Governance Motto several times, thinking that this will immediately give me enough courage to pull my head out of the quilt, but as soon as I touch the cold air outside, I feel that all thoughts are lost, and I shrink my head back in without resistance; from then on, I never recover, and I don't want to get up at all.

Hugging the quilt can of course avoid the temporary cold, but it is not a long-term solution; all the expenses at home have to be earned by myself; if I don't get up one day, I will have to go hungry for one day; then, should we still muster up the courage, lift the quilt, break the temporary cold, and seek permanent comfort?

Our volunteer army, since there was no food, grass, or bullets in the past, and no reinforcements to support them, could not withstand the attacks of the enemy's scientific weapons, and finally collapsed. The so-called anti-Japanese heroes now are either recuperating in the mountains, or shining shoes and pulling rickshaws in Shanghai. What is the difference between this and those who cannot withstand the cold and have to hug the quilt?

Since the Xinhai Revolution, our country has always been plagued by internal and external troubles, fighting and pressing each other, and cannot withstand the economic and military aggression of imperialists. Although it has led to rural bankruptcy and urban collapse, it has not woken up at all until now. What is the difference between this and hugging the quilt and eating temporary peace?

Acting and Living Wu Jiren 224

Society can only be organized when people interact with each other, which is just like the behavior of an acting troupe. A person in society is like a role in an acting troupe. There are sheng, dan, jing, chou, painted faces, and clowns in the troupe. There are good, evil, loyal, and treacherous people in society, so watching a play is like watching a microcosm of society. However, the roles in the acting troupe are assigned by the troupe leader, and the masses in society are determined and expressed by their own behavior.

The best thing to do as a person is to be indifferent to the world, you are you, I am me. If you can't do that, then you have to join society to play a role. But rather than playing a white-faced villain or a heinous clown in society, it is better to play an upright old man with a beard or a romantic and elegant young man. It's more interesting.

Because there are only a few decades in a lifetime, why be so vicious and forcefully plunder to be scolded and despised? It's better to let go and be a dignified man.

There is a kind of person in the world who is often self-smart, "see fierce avoid, see good bully," "see the big Buddha and worship, see the small Buddha and kick," and also adds that he is full of money, pretending to be the richest man in the world, arrogant and tyrannical, using means to deal with friends everywhere, and people let him some, he takes the lead in everything. As the old saying goes, "Man has a thousand plans, but heaven has only one," although those superstitious words are not what people of the 20th century should say, but the Westerners also pay attention to the theory of cause and effect. I come to advise the world, don't go to the end of the road, don't think that you can "sell people" with money, you must know that although the world has become a ghost, justice still exists, I advise you not to be a "clown" again, but to change to a "upright old man with a beard" to play.

Chapter 21 225

Whispered Words of Earnest Advice to Weak Offspring Before the Lamp

Coldly Observing Heroes Below the Mountain with a Walking Stick

The weather was good on this day, and there were quite a few people coming to see the red leaves. Downstairs at the Western Hills Restaurant, twenty or thirty seats were full. Along the cliffside, a flat area held seven or eight cars. Two of the cars even had military flags planted on them. Old Zhao, dragging his jujube wood cane, said softly to Ji Zhi, "Mr. Gan, look, there are so many men and women here. Is there anyone dressed like me, wearing a blue cloth padded jacket and dragging a jujube wood cane?" Ji Zhi laughed and said, "They run the restaurant, we come to spend money. We don't owe them a penny. What right do they have to tell us what to wear?" As he said this, he disregarded everything and walked into the tea area. However, every seat was taken. Walking past them, under a pedestrian bridge, there was a flat, open space, with a hillside behind it and a flower garden in front. There were four rattan chairs and two tea tables, but no one had sat down yet. This was because the view was blocked by a row of trees and hedges, preventing a distant view. One could only turn around and look at the mountain scenery behind the building. Ji Zhi wanted to see the red leaves on the mountain, so he smiled at Old Zhao and said, "People come to see the red leaves, but they don't sit in a place like this. Instead, they squeeze into the dining area to eat Western food and drink coffee. Isn't that a joke? Please, sit down, please sit down!" So, he moved a rattan chair, facing the mountain, and pulled out a handkerchief from his sleeve, constantly dusting off the chair. Old Zhao said, "You're too kind," and sat down as well. The waiter in the restaurant saw that Ji Zhi was wearing a Western suit and had a very generous manner, not like a poor man. So, he came over to prepare tea and snacks, only glancing at Old Zhao a few extra times. Old Zhao reclined on the rattan chair, looking at the opposite mountain. The scattered temples, amidst the sparse trees, were mostly exposed. In the mountain recesses, occasionally one or two red trees were illuminated by the sunlight, very bright and dazzling. Old Zhao pointed and laughed, "That's enough. If the whole mountain was covered in red leaves..." Before he could finish his sentence, a large handful of melon seed shells fell from the sky, scattering all over his head and body. (290)

In recent years, educational funds have not been distributed monthly, and schools often rely on student fees paid at the beginning of the semester to manage. Starting next semester, the provincial schools have been ordered to waive tuition and accommodation fees, and the funds that schools rely on to manage are gone. In addition, the winter vacation this year begins before the Lunar New Year, making it even more difficult to manage finances. It is difficult to cope. Accordingly, I am writing to request that your office consider the actual situation and find a way to raise funds for one month before the winter vacation for each school, and allocate it as soon as possible to meet the urgent need. (The principal of 12,000 yuan is due on February 20th and March 20th) Therefore, funds have always been disbursed monthly.

Measures for Regular Examination of Primary and Secondary School Student Performance by Educational Administrative Organs 230

Yesterday (the 12th), the Ministry of Education announced ten articles of measures for regular examination of the academic performance of students in secondary and primary schools by educational administrative organs at all levels, and at the same time issued a circular to the education departments of all provinces and cities to comply with them, saying, "The examination of the academic performance of students in primary and secondary schools, in addition to the regular examinations held by schools, should also be strictly assessed by educational administrative organs. In peacetime, the method of random examination by branch school and subject is used to measure whether the teaching progress of each subject is appropriate and whether the teaching methods of each subject are appropriate. Then, the results obtained can be used as accurate guidance, in order to improve teaching effectiveness. This is actually more important than regular examinations. We have specially formulated measures for the regular examination of the academic performance of students in secondary and primary schools by educational administrative organs at all levels, and ordered them to be sent to the relevant departments for strict compliance starting from this semester, and to instruct all subordinates to comply with them uniformly. The ten articles of the examination measures are as follows:

Article 1: Educational administrative organs at all levels, in order to improve the teaching methods of each subject in secondary and primary schools and improve teaching effectiveness, should use examination methods in peacetime to examine the academic performance of students in the secondary and primary schools under their jurisdiction.

Article 2: Educational administrative organs at all levels may designate schools, classes, or subjects at any time for the secondary and primary schools under their jurisdiction to conduct examinations. However, before the examination is conducted, the schools, classes, subjects, and dates of the examination should not be announced.

Article 3: The examination of the regular academic performance of students in provincial, municipal, and county-level secondary schools and approved private secondary schools, as well as provincial primary school students, shall be presided over by the Education Department and may designate school faculty and staff to assist in it. When necessary, the provincial Education Department may order the county and municipal educational administrative organs to handle it. The examination of the regular academic performance of students in county and municipal-level and approved private primary schools shall be presided over by the county and municipal educational administrative organs and may designate school faculty and staff to assist in it. When necessary, it may be handled directly by the Education Department. The examination of the regular academic performance of students in public and private secondary and primary schools in the municipal (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan) districts shall be presided over by the municipal district educational administrative organs and shall be designated to assist the faculty and staff of the school.

Article 4: Each provincial, municipal, and district educational administrative organ shall conduct this examination at least once per academic year for the secondary school students under its jurisdiction. Each county and municipal educational administrative organ shall conduct this examination at least once per semester for the primary school students under its jurisdiction.

Article 5: When educational administrative organs at all levels conduct this examination, they should pay special attention to: 1) Junior middle schools that did not participate in the graduation examination last year; 2) Subjects with poor examination results; 3) Subjects that have not been examined in senior and junior high schools.

Article 6: Schools with strict regular examinations and excellent results may be exempted from this examination at the discretion of the competent educational administrative organ, but schools may not request to hold student examinations for the semester on their own. Public and private secondary and primary school students in places where student examinations are not held may be exempted from this examination.

Article 7: For the examination of subjects such as physical fitness and labor, which cannot be applied to written examinations, the competent educational administrative organ shall formulate separate measures for examination.

Article 8: The question-making method and the method of calculating grades for this examination shall be formulated in detail by the educational administrative organs at all levels and submitted to the higher-level educational administrative organ for record.

Article 9: The results of this examination shall be announced within one month after the end of the examination, and a report shall be prepared, proposing a plan for improvement in teaching, and submitted to the higher-level educational administrative organ for review and record.

Article 10: These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

League of Nations Educational Films Come to China 232

The International Educational Film Association of Rome, Italy, is the hub of international educational films. All educational films produced by various countries that have been reviewed and approved by the Association are called International Educational Films and can be circulated in various countries. Therefore, the educational films produced or managed by the Association are exceptionally excellent. The China Educational Film Association, in order to promote communication between Chinese and Western educational cultures, has specially ordered various educational films from the Association. The first batch of films has been shipped from Rome to Shanghai, including twelve films totaling 35 kilometers, such as Historical Rome, Eye Surgery, Tree Oil, Steel, Flowing Gas, Common Lung Diseases, From Egg to Chicken, and Ancient Black Gilt Lamps, worth a total of 12,158.10 Italian currency, with a total length of more than 5,000 feet, rich in content, and quite interesting. The second batch of films is said to be on the way, but these films all have Italian subtitles, which inevitably causes a gap for the audience. The China Educational Film Association is currently engaged in translating the subtitles and will release them to the public soon. Schools at all levels and social education institutions in our country are welcome to contact the association for screenings.

The Bureau of Social Education and the Bureau of Labor jointly announced the Implementation Rules for Municipal Labor Education 237

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Education and the Bureau of Labor announced that the General Outline of the Implementation Measures for Labor Education in Shanghai and its Implementation Rules have been jointly drafted by the Bureau of Social Education and the Bureau of Labor, and submitted to the Municipal Government for instructions. With the approval of the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Education, the Rules are now copied and announced for public knowledge.

General Outline of the Implementation Measures for Labor Education in Shanghai and its Implementation Rules

Article 1: These Implementation Rules are formulated in accordance with Article 17 of the General Outline of the Implementation Measures for Labor Education promulgated by the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Education.

Article 2: Labor education is divided into three types: literacy training, civic training, and vocational training. All workers in factories, companies, and shops in the city should enter labor schools or labor classes to receive various training. However, those who have one of the following circumstances may be exempted from part of the training: 1) Those who have graduated from public schools or other equivalent schools and have a graduation certificate may be exempted from literacy training; 2) Those who have passed the literacy test may be exempted from literacy training; 3) Those who have passed the civic training test may be exempted from civic training; 4) Those who have passed the vocational training test may be exempted from vocational training. The literacy and civic training tests will be held by the Education Bureau in conjunction with the Social Bureau one month before the start of each semester. The vocational training test will be held by each factory as needed, but the test results must be submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau for review.

Article 3: Factories, companies, shops, etc. in the city that employ 50 or more workers should establish labor schools or labor classes. However, if there are fewer than 30 workers who should receive the same type of training, they may send workers to municipal or private labor schools or labor classes attached to other schools. Factories, companies, and shops that employ fewer than 50 workers should send workers, etc. to municipal or private labor schools or labor classes attached to other schools.

Article 4: In accordance with the provisions of the preceding article, factories, companies, shops, etc. that should establish labor schools or labor classes should fill out two copies of the form, stating the date of preparation, the name, age, place of origin, address, and experience of the preparer, and submit them to the Education Bureau for review and transfer to the Social Bureau within two months from the date of opening. Those who opened before the implementation of these Implementation Rules should prepare to establish labor schools or labor classes within two months from the date of implementation of these Implementation Rules, and complete the previous procedures.

Article 5: Labor schools or labor classes should complete the preparation within two months from the date of submission of the preparation, and must fill out two copies of the application form, stating the following items, together with two copies of the articles of association and rules, and submit them to the Education Bureau for joint approval by the Social Bureau before opening: 1) School name and address; 2) Preparation process; 3) Overview of expenses; 4) Curriculum vitae of faculty and staff; 5) Overview of equipment; 6) Number of classes; 7) Opening date.

Article 6: Within one month from the date of opening of the labor school or labor class, the original establishing agency should fill out two copies of the application registration form, stating the following items, together with two copies of the articles of association and rules, and submit them to the Education Bureau for joint approval by the Social Bureau: 1) School name and address; 2) Name and address of the original establishing agency; 3) Curriculum vitae of faculty and staff; 4) Overview of expenses; 5) Overview of equipment; 6) Outline of subjects and curricula; 7) Number of classes and students. Labor schools or labor classes established before the implementation of these Implementation Rules should apply for registration within two months after the implementation of these Implementation Rules.

Article 7: At the end of each semester, labor schools or labor classes should fill out five copies of the report form, stating the following items, and submit them to the Education Bureau for review and transfer to the Social Bureau, and submit them to the Municipal Government for consultation with the Ministry of Industry and Education for record: 1) School name and address; 2) Name and address of the original establishing agency; 3) Curriculum vitae of faculty and staff; 4) Income and expenditure of expenses; 5) Number of classes and students; 6) Number of new students and graduates; 7) Total class hours; 8) Student attendance; 9) Other.

Article 8: When students of labor schools or labor classes complete their studies, they must submit their grades to the Education Bureau for review, and submit their certificates to the Bureau for stamping.

Article 9: The teaching subjects of labor schools or labor classes are as follows: 1) For those who are literate, the Three Principles of the People Thousand-Character Class, Common Sense, Abacus or Pen Calculation, Music and Songs, and Writing. In addition, history, geography, nature, and other simple readings may be taught; 2) For those who are trained in citizenship, the Three Principles of the People, a Brief Introduction to Local Autonomy, the General Situation of the Country, Civic Morality, Labor Organization, and Labor Undertakings. The subjects listed above may be taught to students by lectures and simple readings, and students may be guided to organize various gatherings and implement practical training outside of class; 3) For vocational training, service ethics, general knowledge of agriculture, industry and commerce, and specialized vocational knowledge and skills (to be established according to the needs of workers in various industries).

Article 10: In addition to teaching the subjects in the preceding article, labor schools or labor classes should also take into account extracurricular life, and hold lectures, parties, and exhibitions.

Article 11: The teaching materials of labor schools or labor classes, in addition to the Three Principles of the People Thousand-Character Class promulgated by the Ministry of Education as the basic teaching material for literacy training, may be selected by the teachers themselves, but must be submitted to the Education Bureau for approval.

Article 12: The teaching of labor schools or labor classes must be outside of working hours, at least eight hours per week per class. The training period for literacy and civic training is one year, but vocational training may be extended to two years as appropriate.

Article 13: Students of labor schools or labor classes who pass the examination at the end of the training period of each type of training will be given a certificate by the school or the original establishing agency, and those with excellent grades will be given appropriate awards.

Article 14: Labor schools or labor classes should provide extracurricular study guidance for graduates, and try to provide them with self-study teaching materials as much as possible.

Article 15: The principal of the labor school or the director and teachers of the labor class are hired by the original establishing agency and reported to the Municipal Education Bureau for record. Article 16: Students of labor schools or labor classes who are absent from class without reason will be treated as absent from work without reason.

Article 17: The principal of the labor school or the director and teachers of the labor class should meet one of the following qualifications: 1) Principal or Director: A, those who are employed in the original establishing agency and have educational experience; B, those who have graduated from senior high school or old-style middle school; 2) Literacy training teacher: A, those who have graduated from junior high school or have the same level; 3) Civic training teacher: A, those who have graduated from secondary school and have considerable research in social science; 4) Vocational training teacher: A, general subjects must have one of the qualifications listed in the above three items; B, specialized subjects must have specialized knowledge or skills. The teachers in the preceding item, except for those who teach specialized subjects, should be full-time in principle.

Article 10: The salary standards for faculty and staff of labor schools or labor classes are as follows: 1) The principal's salary is at least 40 yuan per month; 2) The director's salary is at least 35 yuan per month; 3) The teacher's salary is at least 30 yuan per month for full-time. The principal or director and teachers, if they are concurrently employed by the staff of the original establishing agency, should be volunteer, but may be given a commuting allowance.

Article 19: The expenses of labor schools or labor classes shall be borne by the original establishing agency.

Article 20: Labor schools or labor classes do not charge tuition or other fees. All books, stationery, etc. are provided by the labor school or labor class or the original establishing agency.

Article 21: All factories, public stores, etc. in the city that do not establish labor schools or labor classes within the time limit stipulated in these Implementation Rules shall be fined up to 100 yuan, and shall still be ordered to prepare and establish them within two months.

Article 22: These Implementation Rules may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered.

Article 23: These Implementation Rules shall be submitted to the Municipal Government for consultation with the Ministry of Industry and Education for approval before implementation.

Meetings of the Standing Committee and the Security Department

The Rules of Procedure for the Security Department were adopted

The Shanghai Children's Welfare Association is a permanent organization that seeks the welfare of children throughout the city. The Public Security Bureau would be responsible for 1,000 yuan in expenses, and Wang Yiting would contribute 500 yuan from charitable organizations. Expansion or not would be determined based on the results after three months. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Detailed Rules of Procedure 241

Detailed Rules of Procedure for the Protection Department:

Article 1: These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 3, Section 2 of the Association's Articles of Association.

Article 2: All matters handled by this department shall be governed by these detailed rules, unless otherwise provided in the Association's Articles of Association.

Article 3: This department is organized by a Director and several committee members.

Article 4: In addition to the above committee members, this department may petition the committee to appoint three to five enthusiastic children's welfare advocates as supporting committee members.

Article 5: All committee members of this department are honorary positions.

Article 6: The Director of this department, under the command of the President and the Committee of the Association, shall oversee all matters of this department and supervise all groups under its jurisdiction in handling all matters.

Article 7: The committee members of this department shall assist the Director in handling all matters.

Article 8: This department shall have several staff members, who shall be recommended by the Director, approved by the Standing Committee of the Association, and appointed or commissioned by the President of the Association.

Article 9: This department shall have two groups: an investigation group and a relief group, which shall handle various matters separately.

Article 10: This department shall have two group leaders, who shall be elected by the committee members.

(A) Matters handled by the Investigation Group:

(1) Matters related to investigating the treatment of child laborers.

(2) Matters related to investigating abused children.

(3) Matters related to investigating slave rearing.

(4) Other investigation matters.

(B) Matters handled by the Relief Group:

(1) Matters related to rescuing abducted children.

(2) Matters related to rescuing vagrant children.

(3) Matters related to rescuing abandoned children.

(4) Matters related to finding ways to protect the safety of children outdoors.

(5) Other relief matters.

Article 11: The expenses of this department are divided into startup costs and recurring costs. The startup costs shall be submitted to the committee for approval and appropriation. The recurring costs shall be raised separately by the committee members of this department. However, the funds raised shall be used exclusively for this department to handle various matters. The verification and safekeeping of all funds shall be handled by the Committee of the Association.

Article 12: The Committee of this department shall convene a regular meeting once a month. When necessary, the Director may convene an extraordinary meeting.

Article 13: This department shall hold a staff meeting once a week, which shall be convened in rotation by the group leaders of each group. When necessary, an extraordinary meeting may be convened.

Article 14: These detailed rules shall be implemented after being approved by the Committee meeting of this department and approved by the President of the Association. If there are any matters not covered, they may be submitted for amendment at any time.

Therefore, they have established a securities industry primary school at 15 and 16 Wangjia Sha Huayuan Road. With sufficient funding and comprehensive facilities, the teachers hired are strictly selected, tuition is low, and the school provides for both the poor and the genders separately, with dormitories available. These are the school's characteristics. The school will open soon, and its benefits to society will be significant.

As the current semester begins, the school is expanding its facilities. Ms. Wang Yan's Invention of Tennis Game Methods (Continued) 259

Similar to volleyball, it is very suitable for the elderly and women.

Legal Set Ball: A set ball is considered legal if it completely meets the following four conditions: (1) Each person must not set twice or more in a row (when setting with both hands, it is illegal if it is not lifted at the same time, or if it is set twice in a row with one hand, or if the sounds are inconsistent, and it is considered two or more consecutive sets); (2) The ball must not be paused in the palm of the hand; (3) When teammates on each side pass the set ball in the air within their own area, it must not exceed three times or be picked up again after landing (but if the ball falls on the net and does not pass through or land, it can be increased to four times); (4) Teammates setting the ball must stand in a legal area.

Rules During Attack and Defense 260

(1) During an attack, all players on both sides must not touch any part of the net or basket; (2) When a player jumps up and lands again, their feet must not cross the horizontal line under the net; (3) Players must not stand beyond the horizontal line; (4) When a player attacks, they may extend their hands or any part of their body over the top of the net to prevent the ball from entering the basket.

(5) Victory

The victory of this game is determined by the side that first scores twenty-two points. The victory of a match is determined by winning three of five sets. Every set, whichever side scores eleven points first, the sides switch positions once. (Note: The ball used for tennis can be replaced by a volleyball.)

(6) Appendix

The above rules have three special points. The reasons for them are explained as follows: (1) Rules During Attack and Defense, (4) Players may extend their hands over the top of the net during an attack (detailed earlier). This rule is a method to defend against balls entering the basket, because if it is not allowed to extend hands over the net, there will be no way to prevent the opponent from setting the ball into the basket; (2) Scoring, (6) Players intentionally commit fouls and lose two points (detailed earlier). The purpose of this rule is to avoid players from taking advantage. Because if Party A is attacking the ball into the basket and Party B commits a foul, moving the net basket to avoid the ball entering the basket, and the foul is still punished as an ordinary foul and counted as one point of failure, then Party A originally had the opportunity to score two points, but now only gets one point, which is quite unfair. Therefore, Rule (6) stipulates that they win two points, and the decision of this rule is up to the referee at the time. The referee should base on the above spirit to judge and must not arbitrarily decide that a certain party's ordinary foul is an intentional foul; (3) The second provision of the venue stipulates that the rectangle is moved, and the net height is two meters (two meters fifty for men) to avoid the fierce attack of spiking. Therefore, it is suitable for the physique of women. (End)

Shen Bao Wireless Radio Weekly

Circuit for Measuring Audio Frequency Amplification 262

— Wang Xuansheng

After a radio wave is converted into an audio frequency by a detector in a radio receiver and then amplified by a vacuum tube, its volume can be increased several times. The following circuit can be used to measure the amplification value.

In the diagram, the resistors R1 and R2 should be equal in value, and their value can be up to 10,000 ohms. R is a lower resistance, the magnitude of its value depends on the voltage supplied by the audio frequency alternator and the determined signal strength. r is a linear or circular sliding resistor. As shown in the figure, move the DPDT switch to the left, the earphones are connected via R, and when moved to the right, the earphones are connected to the output of the amplifier.

The measurement method is a comparative method, which compares the signal in the earphones when connected via R with the signal produced by the amplifier when connected via r.

The alternator is configured to the required voltage and frequency. The voltage is often configured to about 5 volts. The frequency can be adjusted to the determined frequency band. Draw an amplification curve to represent the frequency. Traditionally, 1000 cycles are often used to simplify the measurement.

After the signal strength has been adjusted by the resistors R1 and R2, the switch is moved back and forth, and the value of r is changed at the same time, until the same signal strength can be obtained in the earphones when the switch is in the front and rear positions. Because the resistors are in series, the current flowing through both sides is the same value. The voltage is proportional to the resistance; therefore, the ratio of the voltage passing through the earphones to the voltage input to the amplifier is equal to the ratio of R to r. Therefore, when the switch is in the front and rear positions and the signals are the same, its

Voltage amplification = R - r

To reduce any residual signal generated by coupling capacitance, one end of the slider and one side of the amplifier input can be grounded.

Example:

Suppose that in a certain measurement, R1 and R2 are 5000 ohms, R is 20 ohms, and r is 0.95 ohms, find the amplification value.

Solution:

R1 = R2 = 5000 Ohm

R = 20 Ohm

r = 0.95 Ohm

Formula

Voltage Amplification = R - r = 20 - 0.95 = 21.0

Voltage Amplification = 21.0 (End)

Earphones 263

Loudspeaker Protection Method 264

— Li Yuanqing

In the final stage low-frequency amplification of radios, if powerful vacuum tubes are used, such tubes have especially large screen currents. If the loudspeaker is connected in series within the screen circuit, it is often easily damaged. To avoid losses, we must consider protective methods:

Figure 2

Figure 1

(1) As shown in Figure 1, L is a low-frequency choke coil, connected in series in the screen circuit. The loudspeaker is connected in series with a fixed capacitor and then connected in parallel across the choke coil. This way, no screen current passes through the loudspeaker, but the oscillating low-frequency waves still pass through normally.

(2) Because in the first method, one terminal of the loudspeaker is directly connected to the high-voltage B supply, it is very easy to get an electric shock if one is not careful when using it. There are two ways to remedy this:

a. Add a fixed capacitor with the same capacitance as C at point X.

b. Instead of adding a capacitor, directly connect the X wire to the ground wire (as shown by the dashed line in the figure).

(3) Without using a choke coil and capacitor, a single output transformer can also protect the loudspeaker.

Regardless of which protection method is used, the most important thing is that the AC resistance of L must be equal to the AC resistance of the final stage vacuum tube's screen electrode to obtain the maximum output power. If you want to obtain the maximum undistorted output power, then the AC resistance of L should be twice the AC resistance of the screen electrode.

Small Experiences 265

— Shi Jia'an

(1) Simple Method for Identifying Current Polarity

To distinguish the positive and negative poles of a current, polarity test paper is usually used, which was introduced in issue 42 of this publication. This article introduces several simple methods that readers can try:

(1) Take a sweet potato, cut it in half at the waist, insert the positive and negative wires, and after a while, observe the color next to the two wires: the one with a purple-green color is the positive polarity; the one with no effect is the negative polarity.

(2) Add edible salt to a cup of water, insert the two wires, and the electrode with bubbles attached is the negative electrode; conversely, it is the positive electrode.

(3) For low-voltage wires, the positive and negative poles can also be distinguished with the tongue: when the wire touches the tip of the tongue, the one that feels slightly numb and itchy is the positive electrode; the one with no taste is the negative electrode.

(2) Ready-Made Antenna

This publication has already introduced how to use telephone lines and electric light wires as antennas. Now there is another type of ready-made antenna: the author once used a roof gutter as an antenna, connecting the lead-in wire to the part of the gutter that runs parallel to the roof, and the reception was also not bad.

(3) Using Carbon to Make a Crystal Detector

Take out the carbon rod from a discarded battery, crush it, select the more regular ones and soak them in a lead acetate (obtained by dissolving lead or lead monoxide in acetic acid) solution for a few minutes. Then, take it out and sprinkle calcium sulfide on all parts of the carbon, and then apply sulfuric acid to the surface.

Common Knowledge

(23) Vacuum Tube Detector 268

— Huang Jiancun

(1) Vacuum Tube Detection: Regardless of the type of radio, it must have a detection circuit to convert the radio frequency current received by the antenna into an audio frequency current. Vacuum tubes have a rectifying effect, so they can be used for detection. A radio that uses a vacuum tube for detection is called a vacuum tube detection radio. The commonly called "one-tube radio" belongs to this category.

There are two different methods of vacuum tube detection: one is the so-called grid leak detection (Grid Detection), which uses a grid leak resistor (GridLeak) and a grid capacitor (GrjdCondenser) for detection, and the other is the plate detection (PlateDetectjoo), which does not use a grid leak resistor or a grid capacitor, but uses a C battery.

(2) Plate Detection: The plate current of a vacuum tube, like a crystal detector, has a unidirectional characteristic. Plate detection utilizes this characteristic to perform detection. Figure 1 shows its standard connection method. By appropriately increasing or decreasing the C battery, the plate current is brought close to zero. At this time, if a high-frequency voltage is generated in the tuned circuit, the positive voltage in it will cause the plate current to flow, thereby achieving the purpose of detection.

Figure 2

Figure 1

(3) Grid Detection: Figure 2 shows the connection method of grid detection. The most important thing is to use the so-called unidirectional property of the grid current between the grid and the filament to perform the detection function. When the grid voltage is positive, there is grid current flowing between the grid and the filament; conversely, if the grid voltage is negative, there is no grid current. Therefore, when a high-frequency voltage is generated in the tuned circuit, if the voltage is positive, grid current will flow. As a result, an audio voltage will inevitably be generated across the grid leak resistor (Rg) and the grid capacitor (Cg). This audio voltage is amplified and generated in the plate circuit, and then becomes an audio current flowing into the headphones. In this method, the vacuum tube serves both detection and amplification functions.

(4) Comparison of the Two Detection Methods: The two detection methods mentioned above each have their advantages and disadvantages. Which is better cannot be generalized. However, grid detection has better sensitivity and is used by many. A table comparing the advantages and disadvantages of the two is given below.

Shanghai Chinese and English Cotton Yarn Stock Statistics at the End of December 281

Total: 138,925 Bales

Increase of 15,362 Bales Compared to Last Month

According to a survey by a Japanese trading company, the total cotton yarn inventory in Shanghai at the end of December of the 22nd year [of the Republic] amounted to 138,925 bales, an increase of 15,362 bales compared to the end of November. Among them, Japanese yarn accounted for 15,685 bales, an increase of 6,932 bales compared to the end of November, while Chinese and English yarn accounted for 123,240 bales, an increase of 8,430 bales compared to the end of November. The reason for the increase in cotton yarn is attributed to the independence of Fujian, the unstable political situation, the sluggish public sentiment, the tightening of finance, the dull sales in various regions, and the collapse of Osaka Sanpin yarn, which greatly affected exports. The breakdown of Japanese factory yarn stocks is listed below:

8-count: 125, 16-count: 2,040, 40-count: 1,860

10-count: 250, 20-count: 4,895, 42-count: 1,990

60-count: 500, 32-count: 4,000, 80-count: 25

Total: 15,685 bales

Uniform Rise in Foreign Cotton Prices 282

Yesterday's U.S. cotton market initially rose due to good news from Liverpool and buying by traders, but later weakened as some bulls took profits. As a result, spot prices rose by 5 points, and futures prices rose by 4 to 8 points. Liverpool cotton spot prices rose by 13 points, and futures prices rose by 89 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 20 points. The Bombay cotton market rose due to buying by European exporters and speculators. As a result, Pingal rose by 1.5 rupees, Oomra rose by 1.75 rupees, and White Rawxi rose by 2.5 rupees. Original telegram on the left (dated the 11th).

Grains

Tianjin Group Sells Standard Flour 283

After the opening of the flour market this morning, the market for each month continued to show a bullish trend. Although the price of foreign wheat from Chicago was down by about four or five jiao, Canadian wheat remained unchanged. However, market sentiment was naturally good as factories were actively purchasing near-term flour. Furthermore, the Taizihdao group had some spot flour transactions, which further boosted confidence. This month's price had risen as high as 1 jiao 6 fen, and February also showed a slight increase of nearly 1 fen. However, the Tianjin group continued to sell, so the remaining months remained flat. Until the afternoon opening, due to rumors of factories selling back, this month's prices also saw some selling. The Tianjin group's persistent selling caused market sentiment to decline step by step. (It is said that the spot price in Tianjin is only 2 yuan 2 jiao 5 or 6 fen), and the decline was quite significant. As a result, this month's price fell by a small 5 li, February fell by 1 fen, March fell by 1 fen 2.5 li, April fell by 1 fen, and May and June fell by 1.5 fen.

The Quiet Period for Futures Wheat 284

Yesterday's futures wheat market remained generally stable in the morning and afternoon. Although the price of foreign wheat was reported to be down by a small 4 or 5 jiao, there were very few sellers in the market. Outsiders rarely inquired, and those in the trade mostly remained cautious, so transactions were unusually quiet. However, this situation may only see a turnaround after the spring. As a result, February was up by 3 fen, March was up by 1 fen, June was up by 2 fen, and there were no other changes. Spot wheat is scarce in both sales and arrivals, and inventories are also low. Holders are very firm in their thinking, and high-grade wheat is quoted at over 4 yuan 1 jiao.

Large Arrivals of Thick Japonica Rice, Continued Decline of a Few Jiao 285

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, sources from various groups arrived again, totaling about 7,000+ shih of thick japonica and various colored 50-grade rice, and 4-5,000+ shih of late indica 30-grade. Due to the market price already showing a bottoming-out, Hakka merchants intending to purchase the late indica rice were quite enthusiastic at the start of the market, and sellers successively tightened their prices. However, contrary to expectations, the Hakka merchants held different views, resulting in only 4,000+ packages being purchased from groups such as Tanggu, Tianjin, and Weihaiwei. Due to strict inventory clearance, the market price was difficult to rise, remaining in a stable situation. Considering the above, its trend may not be optimistic. The supply of thick japonica and Dujian foreign rice still exceeds demand, lacking the ability to turn around. The market price ultimately fell again by several fen to a jiao or so, and the demand for change dollar was firm.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 64-65 ships arrived from various groups downstream. Sales of various goods in the market were weak. High-grade white japonica and Baiyuan rice were down by a small amount, and medium-grade prices were down by a small jiao. Yangdu and Bujian rice were down by 5 fen. Early thin indica rice also showed a weakening trend, and Hakka merchants were firmly positioned.

Second-Grade Hakka Yuan Rice Opens at Lower Price Due to Price Drops 286

|| Hakka Xian Rice Restocked by Quanzhou||

Yesterday's Hakka Xian rice market was originally expected to decline slightly. Because the prices in this street were relatively reasonable, purchases continued. The Min province side [Fujian] still did not restock due to the unstable political situation, but the Quanzhou group inquired about it while the prices were low. Market sentiment stabilized slightly, and market prices also stabilized. In the future, if the appetites of the Hakka merchants are strong again, the market may turn around. Because the current inventory and arrivals are both low, once the major groups purchase actively, the market can recover immediately. The total sales for the day included 100 packages of Hunan machine-processed oil rice at 7 yuan 2 jiao 7 fen, 300 packages of Pijing rice at 5 yuan 8 jiao 7 fen to 5 yuan 8 jiao, and 287 packages of Nanjing factory machine-processed Xian rice. The Beijing Xian rice was purchased by the Quanzhou group, and the rest were purchased by this street. This year's rice harvest was abundant, especially glutinous rice. Most of the glutinous rice goes to consumption in the production of wine, industry, tea shops, and Cifan vendors, etc., and is not as essential to daily life as japonica and indica rice. In recent years, the political situation and economy have deteriorated, and consumption has naturally decreased, so the price of Yuan rice has declined and is lower than the price of japonica rice. Recently, in addition to arrivals from downstream, Hakka Yuan rice arriving in Shanghai is also plentiful. The other day, 800+ packages of newly arrived Jiangxi second-grade machine-processed Yuan rice attracted little attention. Yesterday, this street purchased 53 packages, reduced to 6 yuan 5 jiao, 2 jiao 5 fen lower than the previous market price and half a yuan lower than last month. The selling price of high-grade Hakka Yuan rice remained high. Yesterday, Yutai allocated 30 packages of Hunan high-grade machine-processed Yuan rice to rice shops in this street at a price of 7 or 8 yuan 8 jiao, but the sales channels are different, and the selling price ultimately refuses to go down.

Soybean Sales Are Quite Active 287

Yesterday, soybean sales were quite active. Factories purchased 11-12 truckloads, inland truckers purchased 3-4 truckloads, and this street purchased 3 truckloads.

Exports to Ningbo and Fuzhou need to purchase 2-300 packages, and the price is slightly up by 3-4 fen compared to the previous day.
