Oil Market

Hankou Tung Oil Rises and Then Falls Back 289

Recently, white tung oil has seen a continued rise due to active sales by foreign firms in Hankou, rising from 23 yuan to 24 yuan 5 jiao. However, after the price increase, foreign firms stationed in Hankou adopted a wait-and-see attitude, so the transaction volume decreased. Each time the market opened, only 20-30 tons were traded, indicating that the foreign firms' minds were not settled and the Hankou traders' desires were not satisfied, wanting to take the opportunity to add 25 yuan. As detailed in the previous day's Hankou letter, there was a trend of opening at 25 yuan, but in reality, it did not open. However, yesterday's letter suddenly deteriorated, and the Hankou traders expressed a willingness to sell to foreign firms at 24 yuan. Although there was no transaction, the sharp turnaround in market conditions is undeniable. According to information from the Sichuan and Hunan routes, arrivals will be strong, and it is said that many goods are being shipped out. Hankou is a central gathering place, and when they all arrive, the quantity will be considerable. The other day, Hankou traders purchased Xiang Tung oil at 19 yuan 5 jiao and South Branch including tax at 19 yuan 3 or 4 jiao, all custom orders, totaling 2-3,000 dan. Judging from the current market, this price may be stable, but it still depends on the prosperity of foreign sales. As for Zhejiang tung oil, in the past few days, seeing a turnaround in the Hankou market, the market also echoed, increasing from 19 yuan 7 or 8 jiao for delivery in Shanghai to 20 yuan 078 jiao. Hangzhou traders sold in Shanghai, also in the range of 2-3,000 dan. Therefore, the recent inventory of each oil and hemp shop is no longer as thin as it was a week ago, and it is evident that the market has turned from rising to loosening, and all have a trend of ending purchases. Furthermore, arrivals in Hangzhou have continued to be strong recently, as various producing areas in eastern Zhejiang, seeing the market price rise, all want to sell and are rushing to transport goods to Hangzhou to try to sell quickly. The provincial capital is the commercial center of Zhejiang, so it is appropriate that the sources are increasing daily.

Metals

The Price of Pure Antimony Continues to Decline 290

Recently, Hunan pure antimony has been sluggish due to the cold business of foreign firms and the scarce demand from local mints and arsenals in various ports. However, arrivals have been very strong, resulting in extremely thick accumulation, extremely soft sentiment, and a weak market. Therefore, market prices are gradually loosening, and the overall market situation is also showing a downward trend. The recent estimated price is 300 yuan per ton, down another 5 yuan from before. It is said that for large-volume transactions and continuous dumping, the market price may be even lower.

Silk Market

Reduced Consumption of Raw Silk in Europe and America 291

The prosperous sales of high-grade Chefoo spun silk produced in Zhejiang and Huguang, which used to be sold through the U.S., have plummeted ever since Japanese silk has been competing at low prices in the U.S. and rayon has been dumped on the market. Last winter, U.S. firms did not purchase any dry spun or big spun silk, and there have been no shipments to the U.S. in the past month. From this, it can be seen that Chefoo spun silk is almost extinct in the U.S. market.

Difficult Turnaround in European and American Silk Sales Most of the European and American silk weaving industries suffered losses last year, and inventories piled up with no one inquiring. This year, they are all focusing on tightening policies, reducing production, and reducing raw silk consumption. The silk inventories in New York and Lyon are still thick, and factory sales are stagnant. Telegrams from thread mills are not converting, and the market in Shanghai is sluggish. Yesterday, only Indian firms purchased 15 packages of coarse yellow and white silk, and prices remained flat and weak.

Free Talk

On Change 314

— Yu Yang

D. Vries believes that the variation of organisms can be divided into two types: one is "hesitant variation" and the other is "sudden variation." The former does not transmit its characteristics to its descendants, so it is not related to the evolution of organisms. The evolution of organisms depends entirely on "sudden string variation" because this is what transmits characteristics to descendants. This theory has been proven by other biologists to be not entirely correct. The so-called "hesitant variation" and "sudden variation" are actually the same thing with only differences in degree.

But no matter how you say it, organisms are always changing, and whether it is hesitant variation or sudden variation, changing back and forth, they will never change back to their old appearance.

This is very different from the transformations of monsters.

Gods and monsters can all transform. For example, the monkey spirit Sun Wukong is incredibly powerful and can transform endlessly. He can transform into various human forms, insects, bottles, clear wind, etc. However, all transformations are temporary, and afterward, he must return to his original form. Moreover, he suffers from having a very cumbersome tail. Once, when he and Erlang Shen fought and transformed into temples, because he had no place to put his tail, he turned it into a flagpole, but it could only be erected behind the temple, revealing the flaw. Similarly, the White Snake in the Legend of the White Snake, even though she transforms into a woman for a long time, when she gets drunk, she cannot control herself and must reveal her original form, even scaring her lover.

These types of transformations can be said to be diverse sudden variations, but the result is actually the same as no change. This is exactly the same as the transformations of certain humans.

Local tyrants and evil gentry can become ultra-left socialists, corrupt warlords can become revolutionary heroes, actors can become doctors of literature. Among humans, unexpected transformations are particularly numerous, but no matter how they change, how can they shed their original form? Liu Guitang transformed fifty-one times in thirty-three years, but wasn't he still a bandit?

Even in temporary transformations, Sun Wukong felt ashamed when he had to transform into a lewd and cheap bird. This kind of psychology is something humans lack. If necessary, humans are willing to transform into anything, no matter how base or vile.

Transformation is not always evolution; evolution is limited to transformation that does not return to its original form.

Life 315

— Liu Xunyu

It seems that there are two attitudes towards life, and it also seems that there are only these two; the best examples are begging and kidnapping.

In the alley where I live, there are two "regular customers" called beggars who come twice a day, at noon and in the evening. Although they are called beggars, they don't beg or ask for alms. Each time they just stand in the alley for seven or eight minutes. When the maids bring out the leftovers, they go up to them, take the food, pour it into their buckets, and quietly wait while eating for the second maid to bring out the leftovers. They always eat their fill and take half a bucket of leftovers back with them. After my meal, I habitually go out to collect the meal money for the next few days, so I always see them twice a day. Every time I walk from the alley entrance to the bus stop, I always wonder, why do they still want to live? People have the courage to live entirely because they are tempted by "hope." Eating leftovers every day without the slightest intention of improving their lives, what "hope" is still tempting them? They want to live, I cannot solve this question, so I think of myself. Although I don't stand in the alley twice a day, I also go to a certain place twice a day. Although I don't carry a small tin bucket to receive leftovers, I also carry a wallet to hold "wages." How much difference is there in essence between wages and leftovers? Why do I still want to live? What "hope" is there that is more tempting than theirs? Thinking of this, I can't help but laugh, and I come to a conclusion that "greed for life" and "fear of death" are actually caused by the latter.

But it doesn't seem to be entirely true; those who hold the second attitude towards life are the opposite proof. They risk death to seek life; if they can get through it, they live; if they can't, they die. It seems that the air of fearing death is less than greed for life in them. Perhaps there is something wrong with saying it this way; greed for life and fear of death are just two sides of the same coin. But they want to live happily; otherwise, they would rather die; this is the characteristic.

One is to eke out a living while waiting for death, the other is to risk death to seek life; which one is right? It is difficult to say, but the latter is always more lively. Unfortunately, I myself am very rich in the temperament of a beggar. I often just lie in bed, looking up at the ceiling, waiting for some fairy's maid in the sky to pour down leftovers. Half of my life history is also cold as ice.

Conditioned Response 316

— Sheng Huanming

On a drizzly night, I fear hearing calls coming from afar.

If in the fine rain threads that lightly pat the window, someone is shouting in the darkness, I will become uneasy. If this kind of sound is closer, my feelings are less; the further away, the more the calls heard by pricking up my ears and holding my breath make me feel lost.

This is probably what is called a "conditioned response" in psychology.

Every time I encounter this kind of sound, the disheveled appearance of Wu Fu's wife vaguely appears before my eyes.

That was the winter after the flood; Wu Fu's wife's thatched shack had been soaked by the flood to the point of collapse.

"Wu Fu's wife, well, you should repair your thatched shack. If a big wind comes, you might not be able to live in it."

Wu Fu's wife was sitting on a "straw sandal stool" at the slanted doorway, making straw sandals. She hesitated slightly: "Well, it's not a big problem, it's still okay, I plan to repair it next year. I think I can support it for another year or so, right? What do you say, Uncle X!"

People not only have a good impression of her words but also of her in all aspects.

"There are not a few who want to pick up this 'worn-out straw sandal' (note) - she really has integrity. If a widow like her had been in a wealthy family in the former Qing Dynasty, the Emperor would definitely erect a memorial arch for her!"

Among the women, the praise for Wu Fu's wife is different. No matter what, a woman is unwilling or inconvenient to praise another woman's chastity, but everyone is convinced of Wu Fu's wife's "willingness to work." When things get "busy," or when someone throws a feast, they always can't do without calling Wu Fu's wife to help. She is agile and doesn't talk too much. In addition, there is another thing that everyone praises: she doesn't haggle over wages. It's okay if she helps for a day and gets a hundred cash less; even if they give her a little rice, she accepts it with a smile. She is not greedy and is generous and not annoying at all.

However, there is also one thing that makes people feel slightly regretful: every time she comes to help, Wu Fu's wife always has to bring her six-year-old posthumous daughter with her. Although the daughter is well-behaved, people generally think that it is adding another mouth to feed.

However, for her, everything else seems secondary; she must have her daughter by her side.

That winter, someone in the village said that Wu Fu's wife owed Jin Tudi, the big landowner, a large debt. Everyone who heard this was a little lost in Wu Fu's wife, but she calmly argued: "I'm a widow, where would I get that? There's no such thing. I can still work to eat, you see; my clothes were made for me by him six years ago - I don't add any clothes, I should be able to make ends meet with a pair of hands - there's no such thing!" She thought this was a terrible rumor.

However, the matter ultimately couldn't be hidden for long: someone had already seen Jin Tudi's accountant frequenting her home several times.

"If she doesn't owe Jin Tudi's debt, then she must be the one who stole from his accounting room. Hmph, who says it isn't? Is it really that hard to make a living with a pair of hands to feed two mouths?" The "fast-mouthed woman," Widow Yu Gui, sneered.

The public's opinion of Wu Fu's wife was gradually not as good as before. Some people thought that since she owed debt, she would inevitably have to steal. Several families who had called her to help began to have some women check their homes to see if she had taken anything. Although they didn't find anything missing, they had heavily added a bit of distrust towards her. The "fast-mouthed woman" said that she had seen Wu Fu's wife standing at the meat shop in the city. Men, however, thought that Wu Fu's wife should not have borrowed money from Jin Tudi, that King Yama.

In the evening, Wu Fu's wife crept into my house like a shadow. Her face was pale, and her voice was trembling: "Auntie, I - can you lend me some money? Ten yuan, preferably twenty or thirty yuan..."

She finally admitted that she had borrowed Jin Tudi's debt. "Auntie," she said, "it's hard to explain, I borrowed it six years ago. I borrowed it after he died to pay for the funeral. At the time, it was only five yuan, but now, with principal and interest," "- it's thirty-six yuan and eighty cents!" She took another step forward, her pupils gleaming: "Thirty-six yuan and eighty cents - if I don't pay it back, his accountant said they'll take my little Zhen as collateral! You... can you help me out a little..."

My mother's answer made her eyes fall: her face reddened, and she stammered: "...Then, please don't tell anyone else!" She walked out step by step: "You can't even help me with five yuan?..."

"Five yuan!" She turned her pleading eyes back a second time, gesturing.

No one had ever seen Wu Fu's wife look so begging.

Several days later, on a drizzly night, someone was shouting sharply and sadly from afar, it was Wu Fu's wife: she was full of tears, sweat, and rain, her hair was disheveled, her pupils were dilated, her face was blue, or perhaps it could be said to be blue-gray. She pulled up her torn front of her garment and wiped the water off her face: "Oh, I worked so hard just for this little darling, oh, she's gone, hehe, I know - I know, Zhen's father, I know!" She walked away muttering to herself.

"Ah Zhen, ai, where are you? Come back soon..." As she disappeared into the darkness, she shouted with her sad and high-pitched voice.

I stared blankly, at the dim and about-to-die vegetable oil lamp, in the distance: on the other side of the dark drizzle, mixed with the sound of rain, and two or three dogs barking, her call came intermittently, so far away, but so clear, my heart seemed about to sink.

(Note) "Worn-out straw sandal": Marrying a poor widow is called picking up a worn-out straw sandal.

Amusing Analogies (Continued) 317

— Shu

(8)

Let me copy a few more sentences from Xu Qi's writings. In his "Three Letters from Leyuan," he wrote: "Villagers invite guests, piling up fruit and boxes, all the same from every household, knowing what they will bring before they even bring it. Thus, literary quality declines daily, inevitably disgusting those in the know, unlike mixed sand, which, though rough, at least doesn't stink." His amusing analogy is very apt, and it aligns perfectly with my own views. I would rather praise "mixed sand" than flatter those easily "stinking" writings, even if the old master once flaunted his skills and frequently shook his head at my words.

(9)

Ji Dong said, "A few years ago, during the spring in the capital, a certain Mr. Lou Dong wrote a detailed critique of Elder Yushan, nitpicking and leaving no stone unturned. Dong Xu told a guest, 'I came from Shandong and once traveled to Mount Tai, ascending the Peak of Sunrise Viewing. While feeling awestruck, I suddenly had an urgent need to urinate. Descending would take ten li, which was unbearable, so I secretly relieved myself at the side of the peak, fearing severe punishment, but I was fine. Why? The mountain is so vast and high, and many people urinate there; Mount Tai doesn't even notice.' The guest jumped up and cursed loudly. However, yesterday I heard Mr. Wu Meicun praising Dong's words highly." This kind of amusing analogy to scold people truly makes one not know whether to laugh or cry. Among modern writers, only Mr. Lu Xun can reach this level.

(10)

Jiang Fen said, "Although contemporary people's selections of poetry are poor, there are still things worth picking. A lotus flower grows out of foul mud; just pick the lotus flower and leave the foul mud." Looking at the current literary scene, it is truly more foul mud than lotus flowers. We should also select magazines and articles in this way.

(10) (1)

Deng Hanyi criticized those who imitate ancient writers, saying, "Their words are neither modern nor ancient, and their spirit is half-alive, half-dead." The former statement is ordinary, but the latter cannot but make people slap the table and exclaim in admiration. Those who blindly imitate are actually "half-alive, half-dead" in spirit, but unfortunately, no one can express it like Hanyi.

(10) (2)

Zhou Qi told his colleague, "During the Jiayou reign of the Song Dynasty, there were no restrictions on visits, and scholars often rushed to seek favors. One person was known as the 'Fire-Watching Horse,' and another as the 'Day-Traveling God,' meaning they spent their days rushing around. Alas! Now, we must use the 'Day-Traveling God' to also ride the 'Fire-Watching Horse,' what is to be done?" The two amusing analogies are cleverly linked.

Two Brothers (84) 318

— By Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

"But surely you won't deceive me, will you?"

Pierre felt so moved that he almost wanted to embrace and kiss him:

"But I am not deceiving you. I can't find a foothold here at all. I'm going to leave this place as a doctor on a transatlantic mail ship."

"Ah! Mr. Pierre! You once promised to help me live!"

"What can I do? I have to live myself. I don't have a penny to my name."

Marosko repeated:

"This is not good, this is not good, what you are doing. I, I only have starvation ahead of me. At my age, this is the end. This is not good. You abandon a poor old man who came to rely on you. This is not good."

Pierre wanted to explain, defend himself, to reason, to prove that he had no choice; but the Pole would not listen to him at all, he was only indignant at his betrayal, and in the end, he even said those words that undoubtedly hinted at some political events:

"You French, you are not trustworthy."

Then Pierre stood up, this time he was somewhat indignant, and he said to him in a slightly haughty tone:

"Old man Marosko, you are being unreasonable. It takes a strong motivation for someone to decide to do something like I've decided to do; you should understand that. Goodbye then. I hope when I see you again, you will be more reasonable than you are now."

Then he walked out.

"So no one feels a real regret about my leaving the country," he thought to himself.

He searched his mind, he thought of everyone he knew or had ever known, and in the parade of faces passing through his memory, he found the face of the barmaid in the beer hall that made him suspicious of his mother.

He hesitated, he still held an instinctive hatred for her, then, he suddenly decided, he thought, "In any case, she guessed right." So he made his way to the beer hall.

The beer hall happened to be full of customers and smoke. Because it was a holiday, the drinkers—both middle class and workers—were shouting, laughing, and yelling, even the owner himself was serving customers, running from table to table, taking away empty glasses, and bringing back full glasses of foam.

As Pierre found a seat near the counter, he waited, hoping the barmaid would see him and recognize him.

But she ran back and forth in front of him, without looking at him once, her legs wiggling prettily under her short skirt as she hurried.

Finally, he tapped the table with a coin. She came running:

"What do you want, sir?"

Her eyes did not look at him, she was focused on calculating the bills of the customers she was serving.

"What!" he said, "Is this how you greet old friends?"

She glanced at him and said in a hurried voice:

"Ah! It's you. Hello. But I don't have time to chat with you today. Do you want a beer?"

"Yes, a beer."

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

A Writer's Lament 319

— Wu

Originally, the term "writer" seemed to be a more elegant name that people used to call those who peddled their writing skills. It was as if, once someone entered the ranks of writers, they became a remarkable, romantic talent. Therefore, I am quite unsuitable to call myself a writer. However, since I am ultimately someone who sells articles, I might as well pretend to be one. Writers have many hardships, and this is a common sentiment among those in the same profession. Therefore, I might as well lament a bit. – The above is considered an introduction to the topic.

However, a writer's hardships are truly endless and inexhaustible. And if I were to imitate the tone of a woman, where should I even begin?

Under the current social system, everything has become a commodity. Prostitutes sell their bodies, actors sell their voices, socialites sell their love, and writers sell their writing to make a living. Since it is selling, there must be customers, which is an unchanging truth. Therefore, to attract customers, there must be various goods to meet their needs. For example, if a customer wants flirtatious behavior, then a prostitute must try her best to appear charming and lovely. If theatergoers like to see Pan Jinlian teasing Wu Song, then it is not enough for the actor to only know how to perform Baochan serving wine. If rich and powerful patrons want socialites to dance naked for them, then it is not enough for the socialites to only be willing to accompany them to see movies of people bathing and taking off their pants. So, what if noble readers want to read romance novels about nephews loving their aunts, and writers only give them works like "The True Story of Ah Q"? If you are not good at having everything available and fulfilling every request, then you can only tighten your belt and wait to die.

However, it is not easy for a writer to transform into a department store. Some publications want humor, some want Saturday School or Butterfly-Mandarin Duck fiction, some want to be non-reactionary, and some want to be improperly reactionary. Therefore, it is truly impossible for a writer to cater to the needs of various markets.

Furthermore, humor and Saturday School fiction still focus on form, while being improperly reactionary or non-reactionary are the most difficult problems for writers to solve.

Naturally, everyone inevitably has their own thoughts, and writers are even more sensitive people. It is impossible to write without emotion. But in these times, a writer's thoughts, other than being "Chinese style" and "qualified," are mostly hidden within the words. I am unfortunate enough to be a writer, and I am also naturally headstrong and unwilling to "follow the instructions." Therefore, I can only lament to myself late at night and hope that you all do not view it as a prostitute's lament.

Page 22

The Front, Back, and Side of Life 320

— Veteran

Being a person is already difficult, and being a modern person is especially difficult.

However, this is only true for a certain group of people who are serious about everything. In the vast universe, if we truly calculate, intelligent people are in the majority. In the eyes of most intelligent people, being a person is not very difficult, but rather quite convenient. This is because they are very intelligent and can thoroughly understand life. Therefore, every morning when they open the door, they can smoothly deal with everything. As for fools, they must consider this and consider that, what is justice, what is truth, what is reason, what is emotion. Naturally, they will run into walls and be unable to open up a path to life. Therefore, they say being a person is difficult. In reality, the difficulty lies in being foolish, being ignorant of the ways of the world. In more fashionable terms, it is not understanding the trend of reality. Being ignorant of the ways of the world and not understanding the trend is something even village women can understand clearly. Your life should be placed outside the circle. Pinch your nose and go cry. In this vast world, who will pity you?

However, what kind of intelligence do intelligent people actually have? It is not that they truly have some extraordinary intelligence, but simply that they have seen through life. In other words, they have achieved understanding the ways of the world and understanding the trend. The major premise is to grasp "fame" and "profit," and their eyes are fixed on "enjoyment." If they do this, they can be successful in everything and become a prominent figure of the era.

Here, we must bring out three typical ways of being a person: the front, the back, and the side.

The front should logically refer to the bright side, but here it is not. It refers to the side that a person shows to those in higher positions, or at least to those who are slightly better. For example, above a director is a minister, the minister's wife, a deputy minister, the deputy minister's wife. This, the side that the director shows to these people, is what I mean by the front. In fact, the meaning is not so narrow. In short, it is the behavior in front of people of higher status, reputation, and power, that is the front. Here, the first thing you need is a smiling, amiable, and friendly face. Speaking is very simple, just keep responding with "yes, yes, yes." If you also have some ideas you want to express, then at least be sincerely terrified, and that is almost enough. There is no need to elaborate on other things. For example, being as loyal as a tail-wagging guard dog, and flattering loudly, are also necessary conditions, but many have already said so, and the meaning is already clear, so there is no need to repeat it.

Speaking of the back, it has actually been subtly hinted at above. It refers to people of lower status than oneself, such as a master treating a servant, a madam treating a maid, a section chief treating a section member, a director treating subordinates, and so on. Here, you must change the sincere terror into being both respected and strict. Middle-aged people in their twenties and thirties may as well twist their beards and keep a little bit. When sitting, cough dryly two or three times from time to time, and then use the index fingers of both hands to touch the two mustaches. There is no need to elaborate on the meaning, just make the gestures and roll your eyes a few times is enough. If that's not enough, you can say, "Why are you so clueless?" This then leads to "blowing."

Under the dignified, Buddha-like mask, you can close your eyes and just blow, and that will be enough. However, you must be careful not to lightly reveal a penny of the secrets and inside stories, otherwise that would be truly terrible. If the other party chuckles, that would not be fun at all.

The side is between the front and the back, and refers to how to treat people of equal status. You cannot completely apply the treasures of the front, nor can you blindly imitate the full set of the back. However, both can be used for reference, and it is good to use them effectively. For example, if the other party is meeting for the first time, then you must give them a good impression. Your face should be kind and friendly, and you can blow at any time. If they are old friends, then you don't need to, but you should be silent as a cicada in winter. You can open up a dignified face without being too restrained or too dissipated. You must make the other party have a good impression of you. The most taboo here is the misuse of the pure front, which often annoys friends and breaks ties with you.

Night Walk in Jiangwan 321

— Yiming

Jiangwan, this land that has been baptized by the artillery fire of imperialism, I have not come to pay my respects for a long time. Tonight, at the invitation of a friend from Fudan University, I went to see the 15th performance of the Fudan Drama Society. So, after eating dinner, I quickly took a car to visit.

It was not until eight o'clock that the opening was announced.

First came the one-act play "The Boor" by the Russian writer Chekhov. This is a comedy of love, and it is very good in terms of technique, but it is backward in terms of consciousness. In tonight's performance by the society, the technique was also not very good. The two important roles, Elena Popova and Grigory Smirnov, were both performed unsuccessfully. Especially Ms. Wang Caizhi, who played Elena Popova, felt even more stiff, although she had the posture of a widow. Bao Shijun, who played the servant Luka, was very good. As for the effects, the electric bell was not realistic enough.

Next was Ding Xilin's "Oppression." The content of this play really did not show oppression, it was just a coincidence. The effect on stage tonight was still good, partly due to the harmony of the actors and partly due to the success of the technique. The female tenant in this play was played by Ms. Wang Ying. Although Ms. Wang did not perform very well, her experience was a little richer than others. The male tenant was played by Wu Tieyi, who played Grigory Smirnov in "The Boor." His performance in this play was better than in the first play. The worst was the old woman, whose makeup, movements, and speech were all bad. This was perhaps due to the director's inattention.

The third play was "Moonrise." This script has been performed many times in Shanghai. The content is still a little interesting, but it is also too old. Tonight's performance was half a failure. First, Li Zhonglin, who played the role of Person One, failed in his performance because he used the same speech and movements for an old man as for a strong young man. Gu Degang, who played the sheriff, performed passably. The other two policemen also did not have any problems. Second, the effects and lighting failed. The lighting was too bright and too dark, which the stage conditions did not allow. Tonight, they made this mistake. The effect of the boat moving in the water was not well done. Only the speech of the people in the play was seen, but the audience did not know what the boat was doing.

The last play was "John Manly." The content of this play depicts a sailor who went missing. His lover had to marry an old man because of poverty at home. After this woman got married, she could never forget her former lover. Every day, she would smile and sing a song from the heart. As a result, she decided not to think about her former lover (thinking he was dead) and told all her secrets to her husband. But, after she told her husband, she could not forget her former lover again after hearing the roar of the sea. She cried sadly. At this moment, her lover (the sailor) suddenly returned. However, she firmly refused to be with her lover again. Finally, the sailor left sadly. This is a tragic drama of love, and there is not much consciousness. In the performance, Ms. Wang Ying was successful in playing the heroine Therese. Bao Shijun's performance as Zoer was also not bad. The worst was Li Zhonglin, who played John Manly. He made the big mistakes of stage fright and unnaturalness.

After watching these four plays, it was already past eleven o'clock. Under the darkness, I left Jiangwan, where the ruins of the fortress still remained, and returned to the embrace of the metropolis.

"If You Want to Change, Change Immediately" 322

— Shiben

A slogan for opening up a new life!

When the New Year arrives, everyone must cheer up, thinking that as the years are renewed, our human affairs should also be renewed. Therefore, everyone is busy reviewing the past and determining the future. If you think of something you did that was not right in the process, you should renew it this year. Then, there is the swearing of "All things of the past are as if they died yesterday, and all things of the future are as if they were born today" as a sign of resolute determination. For example, a friend of mine likes smoking and gambling. In the New Year, he thought of all the harms of smoking and gambling, so he wanted to change his ways from this year onwards, and swore not to smoke or gamble. However, time passed, and not long after, he was gambling and smoking again. People asked him why his New Year's vows were not working. He would definitely say that this year was awkward because he had smoked once and gambled once during the New Year celebrations, so he had already broken his vow. He would wait until next year to make sure he didn't smoke or gamble. So, next New Year, he would have another "All things of the past are as if they died yesterday, and all things of the future are as if they were born today" swearing. Like this, wasting away year after year, procrastinating, and self-deceiving, there are many, many in society! Hoping for a better next year this year, but next year is still a mess! This is the result of everyone embracing the idea of muddling through and not having the awakening of self-renewal.

Therefore, I say that a person either does not sincerely change their ways, or if they really want to sincerely change their past mistakes, do not have any reservations. It is not necessary to resolve to change from the New Year onwards. You can change at any time, as long as you realize your mistakes, change immediately, without hesitating or wavering from X time onwards or from X day onwards. Because "Time flies and never returns," and "An inch of time is hard to buy with an inch of gold." How can we allow ourselves to waste away the valuable youth in the subconscious of "hesitation" and "wavering"!

"If you want to change, change immediately" is the slogan for opening up a new life that I advocate! Friends! If you are an awakened one who wants to "turn over a new leaf," you don't need to hesitate. Start practicing it today!

In fact, "The Times" does not allow us to hesitate! Written on January 6, 1934.

Please Take Tonics! 323

— Yiqin

Some people diagnose China's ailments and say it is suffering from "collapse." It is appropriate to take tonics for collapse, and this does not even require the title of "Doctor of Medicine" to know. However, although some people are trying their best to inject German-made morphine, it is still ineffective. And now, tonics from Japan have arrived again.

According to this newspaper's report on November 23, recently, due to the lull in our country's boycott movement, Japanese merchants are taking advantage of the opportunity to import inferior goods in large quantities. Recently, a large batch of inferior ginseng has arrived, intending to peddle it to various ginseng and medicine stores in this city. However, because the medicine stores are wary of the precedent of Shen Feng and other eight rice firms selling Japanese rice, they are all taking a wait-and-see attitude and dare not openly sell it.

Heaven pities China, which has suffered from years of floods, droughts, and wars. The countryside is barren, and the people are already unable to make a living. Fortunately, we have already eaten American wheat and received Japanese rice. Now, we are also given tonics. How can we not come back to life!

The enthusiasm of the Japanese is to be only grateful for. They are "suppressing bandits" for us in Rehe, and helping to resolve Feng Yuxiang's troops in Chahar. This is considered surgical treatment. Seizing our four northeastern provinces is considered a "package cure." The January 28th Incident gave the people of Shanghai and even the whole country a dose of iron and blood, and it was also a small cut for the Nineteenth Route Army, which would later become "rebels." Now, we need to take tonics. I think that although the medicine stores are still "taking a wait-and-see attitude," "to refuse repeatedly is to be disrespectful." In the end, they will still accept the order like Japanese rice. It's just that "courtesy demands reciprocity, what do we have to repay them with?"

Complaint 325

— Yafei

Life is inherently depressing and boring. But you have to rely on yourself to work hard and strive, recognize the goal, and determine the direction to work hard and strive! Only then can you find bright and great comfort. But I have gone through so many struggles, and the result is still the same disappointment and sadness!

For the sake of pursuing life, I shamelessly went to various places to seek help and beg for assistance. However, I was met with obstacles everywhere, and in the end, I only received a few contemptuous glances! I was finally surrounded by poverty and sorrow! Alas! Heaven! Why is my fate so bad? My destiny is full of twists and turns; what I encounter is always wrong. The old wounds have not yet healed, and new stimuli come again. Unfortunate me, I encounter unfortunate events everywhere. Thus, a layer of sorrow is heavily covered on my blurred nerves! A painful wound is deeply etched on my weak heart! That unfortunate tragedy attacks my heart again. The terrifying scene is forever indelibly emerging in my brain membrane. Let me suffer all the pain of life, let me taste all the torment of life! Ah! Life! I can only complain here, complaining about everything that has passed:

Ten years of failure; Several years of wandering. Only then do I know how difficult it is to be a person, why bother falling into the mortal world! The present is still like the past; From beginning to end. Fish leap, disliking the sea's narrowness, Birds fly, hating the sky's emptiness. Lodging is like morning dew; Living in the world is like a spring dream! How many lost travelers, Cannot escape a life of failure in the end, Only for the sake of current plans; Walking and wading, harming my remaining body, I live on Mount Tiantai; Counting the falling red every day, If one day the golden lock breaks; A dragon runs out of the shallow abyss, Flying up to the sky; Pushing aside the heavy fog. Old hatreds and new sorrows, when can they end? Busy all day long, this floating life is truly like a dream. A beauty with a tragic fate! I am the poorest of all! Time passes in an instant, The seasons are too hurried, Laboring swallows fly apart; When will we meet again? Wasting time in vain; Embracing Sir Copper Coin in vain! I wish that in life after life, Heaven and earth would last forever, Flying away from the cage! I have tasted all the flavors of life; The bitterness, spiciness, and sourness are all in my heart. This is not beautiful singing; Nor is it a clear poem, I cannot write poetry; I don't know how to sing, I don't know how to fill in lyrics. Here are only the sorrowful sounds of me complaining to those who sympathize.

Amateur Mailbox

Will There Be Future Troubles? 326

Editor:

I am a 21-year-old youth. Last June, through the introduction of relatives and friends, I fell in love with Ms. Chen. Soon, she said, "I was once engaged to Mr. Qu; but both parties were unwilling to fulfill the engagement, and we mutually returned the rings and tokens, and a written cancellation of the engagement was signed." After checking the agreement, the tone was only a piece of draft paper prepared for publication in the newspaper, signed by both parties, with no witnesses' signatures. Her explanation to me here is "Because there were no witnesses at the time of the engagement, there were also no witnesses at the time of the cancellation of the engagement." Now, I suspect that Mr. Qu will not come to disrupt things after I am engaged to her, and are we violating the criminal law? Now I want to find Mr. Qu to sign a new contract, but I don't know where he is.

Because I want to avoid these many future troubles, what is a complete solution? Please teach me in detail. I wish

Your believer

Zhuo An, Lu Zhen

X X X X

Editor's Note: Love is blind, regardless of benefits; If you and Ms. Chen have true love, it is better not to consider these many issues. Because once you find out that there are "future troubles," can you bear to cut her off? You must know that Mr. Qu's whereabouts are currently unknown, how can her future be settled? Those who can bear to cut off are definitely not true love, even if there are no future troubles, it is best not to proceed. As for the questions you asked, there is a solution. Ms. Chen should come forward and apply to the court in the place where the engagement took place, based on the reason that Mr. Qu's whereabouts are unknown, to declare the engagement invalid. That incomplete cancellation agreement can be submitted at the same time; because at least it can serve as an expression of the intentions of both parties!

Novel

Prison Notes (8) 327

— Wheels

My legs, I've had over ten injections to prevent numbness, and eaten about a hundred packets of medicine - two packets a day, over ten packets a week - but even now I still don't know what the disease is or what caused it. Although I have a sort of intuitive understanding, the doctors have never told me.

The longer it goes on, the more my fear increases, and I've lost all hope in the doctors' help!

My father sent tiger bone and papaya wine. I long for wine. There's not a drop of it here, and not a trace of its flavor in the food. It seems every nerve in my body is telling me to have it, every cell is parched, and if I have it every day, I seem to be guaranteed to get better! Wine, wine, wine, I lie awake savoring thoughts of it, and dream of it when I sleep.

When I was outside, I didn't feel that wine had these powers, and I didn't often drink it, nor did I feel any particular interest in it. But now it has this strange, mysterious allure for me! I still can't forget buying a hundred coins' worth of old wine, with half left over, and Zhu and I both drank it and got drunk, our faces red! Where does this current craving come from? It can't be wrong, it can cure my illness! My blood, which is becoming numb, blood which is circulating sluggishly, needs the stimulation of yellow wine! - But the real reason is that I am in this arid desert, and my throat has been parched for so long, that the thirst in my throat has become a thirst in my whole soul, my whole body. In my detailed imagination, I have built up the power of the wine, and this thirst has turned into a complete demand from me. A demand for wine.

The wine has arrived, it is for me, it is in response to my thirst, but in the first section - I must still submit a report to the second section, and only after it is approved can it be issued. A kind of interfering relationship has been inserted between my father and me. And this relationship has made me refuse.

Today, I continued to file a report, the content of which was roughly: "Although there are other medicines to treat the disease, they are ineffective. Although tiger bone and papaya wine is wine, it is medicine. The improved prison should have more good medicines in stock, and when prisoners have no choice but to buy them themselves, they should be issued."

Although this report has been submitted, I became terrified after submitting it. Because in my writing, I have completely refuted the head of the second section. Although the reason for refuting him is justified, at least we prisoners say it is justified. However, according to our experience, it is considered inappropriate to refute a superior with justified reasons, and one can only passively accept. But because I didn't have wine to drink, I wrote it out of a momentary emotional impulse. Oh legs, prepare yourselves for shackles tomorrow!
